1)
The Heavy Burden of Destiny
When people think about whether they like or dislike carrying some burden, a heavy burden, they generally do not like it. You may not know this here, but when you go to places like Asia or Korea, you often see oxen loaded with burdens and yoked to plow the fields. Even horses dislike being ridden for long periods. 
Carrying the burdens assigned to each person is part of life. No one wants to carry a heavy burden. However, can we avoid carrying that burden? If I do not carry it, I must impose it on some animal or someone else. If we do not do that, it is a fact that we cannot see progress in our lives or human existence.
From that perspective, we can say that living our individual lives is also about carrying burdens. Therefore, there can be three types of people: those who carry heavy burdens toward a certain goal, those who carry no burden at all, and those who are indecisive about whether to carry a burden or not. The members of our Unification Church would fall into one of these categories. If we look at countries, the United States would also correspond to one of those three types.
February 19, 1978 (Sunday), Belvedere Training Center (New York, USA).
* This message was also published in the May 1978 issue of <Unification World>.

The Heavy Burden of Destiny
In this light, who will carry the heavy burden? If a certain family has taken on that burden, then both the father and mother must carry it together, and if the grandparents are carrying it, then the children must also share in that burden. If there is someone in that family who refuses to carry the burden, what will happen? If there are five family members and one of them refuses to carry the burden, the four who are carrying it will likely judge that one person. However, if the collective decision of the five is that the one person should not be made to carry the burden, that is a different matter.
If, despite being told not to carry the burden, that person still participates in carrying it, what will happen? There must be a reason for telling them not to carry it. Perhaps they are sick or weak, or there is something wrong with their body. When they are told not to carry it but still do, it indicates that the burden is indeed too heavy for them. In that case, the parents or siblings who are also carrying burdens will likely be more concerned about that weaker family member than about their own burdens.
Even while being weak, if they carry the burden and sweat, giving their all to overcome the difficulties, you must understand that their influence on others grows as they continue to persevere. They will receive all the attention and become an object of admiration and emotional reverence. Parents will think of that child with praise in their hearts, and siblings will do the same.
If, on the other hand, a healthy person can normally carry burdens, no matter how quickly or well they do it, they will not become an object of admiration. They may be seen as admirable, but they will not receive sympathy or pity. Even if the burden is something that should be carried as a family, when someone weak carries it, they receive sympathy. But if that burden is taken on in place of someone else, what happens? In that case, even if the person taking on the burden is weak, they will be regarded as better than their parents, friends, or anyone else. We live our lives carrying such responsibilities. Each person walks their own path in life, but we must carry those burdens.
What kind of person will you be?
So, among the three types of people mentioned earlier—those who should carry burdens, those who hesitate to carry them, and those who refuse to carry them—what type of person should we become? That is the question. What kind of person will you be? Will you be someone who carries heavy burdens throughout your life, someone who hesitates to carry them, or someone who avoids carrying them altogether? "Someone who carries them throughout life." That answer is good. Do you like carrying burdens? "Yes." Do you really like it? "Yes." (Laughter)
You see, if there are burdens to be carried and each family member takes one, when there are both large and small burdens, do you choose to carry the large burden or the small one? Be honest. "I prefer the medium-sized ones." (Laughter) In this regard, no one wants to take on a large burden.
If there is a man and a woman, typically the man is expected to carry the larger burdens while the woman carries the smaller ones. However, if a woman stands before a large burden, what happens? And if a man stands before a small burden? (Laughter) Everyone would say, "Look at that man, oh dear." That's right. If a woman takes on a man's burden and a man takes on a woman's burden, if the man is sick or unable to carry it normally, that is understandable. Those who know will understand.
When we look at all the facts that arise in human life, whether it is centered on people or on heaven, it is the same. If God exists, what kind of being is He? He is like a human. Now, what would God be like? Since God is the same, the movement of His heart regarding avoiding responsibility or taking responsibility from an unfair and abnormal position is just like that of humans, and you must understand this. God is eternal. However, we humans live within the short span of a lifetime.
From this perspective, what if there are thousands and thousands of heavy burdens piled up before God? There are burdens of countless shapes and weights that must be taken to a certain destination. However, there is a deadline for carrying those burdens. If there are burdens that God Himself can carry, then He is indeed carrying them. How will God carry those burdens? Will He start with the large burdens, the small ones, or the medium ones? What do you think? "Starting with the large ones." Do you all agree? That is the issue.
If you have to carry them by a certain date, today is February 19, 1978, right? If you must carry them by this date, would you want to move them all before that date, or just by that date, or after that date? "By the deadline." Of course, you would want to move them before that. If there is a year to do it, you would want to move them within that year. So, how long do you think God would want to take to carry them? (Laughter) If He could do it in a moment, He would want to do it in an hour. You all think, "Ah, the Almighty God can do it in less than an hour, right? He can do it in an instant." Don't you think so? God can handle even the most difficult tasks in an instant.
What about us humans? "Since there are 360 days left, and it is February now, at least ten months are left, so let’s take it slow." What do you think? How about you? Don’t laugh, just answer. What do you think? "If I can’t do it today, I’ll do it tomorrow, if I can’t do it this month, I’ll do it next month, and if I can’t do it this year, I’ll do it next year." Is that how you think? What about you, members of the Unification Church? "Not like that." Do you not think about the ten months left and say, "Don’t come in ten months, I will finish it all today"? Is that how you feel? "Yes." If you wait until ten months are left and then still can’t do it, what will happen?
Now, do you think, "Ah, a person should work for eight hours. I must finish by six o'clock. According to labor laws, I must finish by six o'clock...?" Is that necessary? Before eight o'clock in the morning, even if the sun has risen, do you look at the clock and say, "It is still not eight o'clock, the start time"? Do you think, "Oh, it would be nice to work until it gets dark"? What about you, members of the Unification Church? Should you care whether it is dawn or dark? "Yes." That’s good.
When it comes to carrying burdens, will you carry them without energy, or will you carry them with enthusiasm? Will you carry them while dozing off? There are people dozing off here right now. (Laughter) Some people are excitedly listening to the teacher's words…. (Laughter) Seeing everyone laugh shows that you all understand.
More Sympathy and Attention
Does a person not know the way to succeed? Everyone knows. That is why problems arise. If everyone knows, why can’t they do it? Why can’t they do it? If someone can make it happen and can do it, that person will succeed. Everyone knows how to succeed. Do you know or not? "We know." But why can’t you do it? It is because you cannot control yourself. We must understand that remaining in such a state is the human condition.
In the morning, when all Unification Church members gather, they might think, "Oh, why do we have to come so early? Oh, wouldn’t it be nice to gather at ten o'clock like everyone else? Sunday is a day of rest; let’s take it easy and worship. What is this early morning thing? I want to sleep…. Oh, I see there are 30 minutes left!" They would think like that. Is there anyone who likes that? I know very well. Wouldn’t it be nice to gather around ten in the morning? "No." What do you mean by "no"? Those who laugh at "no"…. (Laughter) Why does Reverend Moon make everyone wake up at five in the morning?
Most people cannot control themselves. Those who can control themselves are a specific few. That is why humans need leaders and supervisors. Do you feel good about that or bad? "What do you mean I need a leader? It’s best to do things my way. Why do I need supervision?" That is what they would think. If left alone, eventually everyone will….
When it comes to carrying burdens, whether you eat before carrying them or not, whether you are dressed or not, you must carry them. Whether you sleep or not, you must carry them. If there are two types of people—one who sleeps while carrying and one who doesn’t—who receives more sympathy and attention? If one person eats while carrying and another goes hungry, who gets more attention? If one person is dressed while carrying and another is in just their underwear, who do you pay more attention to? Do you pay more attention to someone who wants to work normally or to someone who wants to work abnormally? "To the one who wants to work abnormally." You know that the more abnormal they are, the more attention they attract.
As they continue to work without eating or sleeping, trying to keep going, they become more and more astonishing and thought-provoking. Isn’t that right? However, among those working, if everyone is working abnormally without eating, and one person says they want to go home and sleep, what will happen? Who will become the focus of attention? "The one working abnormally." (Laughter) You all know.
Now, if this is something that everyone in the world must do, and a specific person says, "You all take a break; I will do it alone," then all humanity will say, "Ah, what a grateful person." However, if that person complains, "All the people in the world are just making me do this," what will happen? Then they would say, "You brat, who asked you to do it?" If someone quietly takes on the responsibility of everyone, the effect will be one hundred percent. Therefore, it must continue like that until the end.
After finishing all the work, let’s say there is a statue representing the world that says, "Ah, that person worked hard." There are two types of people who speak at such a statue. One says, "You all hated working, so I had no choice but to take on the work." That sounds good. However, if someone says, "This celebration is only natural. You should celebrate me," while asking, "Why did only these people come? Why didn’t all the people of the world come to celebrate?" what will happen? That brat…. Such a person may be popular and well-liked, but they forget everything they did.
Always a Person with the Privilege to Carry the World’s Burdens
On the contrary, if a person who looks shabby and is in terrible condition takes on that responsibility and says, "Ah, I am grateful that you all came. If you hadn’t entrusted this work to me, I wouldn’t have had this glory today," what will happen? "I was worried that you wouldn’t entrust the work to me, and I am thankful for being entrusted with it, which allowed me to have today’s glory." This is a world of difference. (Applause)
When we think about this, there are burdens of destiny that we cannot avoid carrying in our lives. Centered around your family, if you belong to the Kim family, then the Kim family has burdens of destiny. Furthermore, if it is a nation, the United States also carries burdens of destiny. This is true for everyone. However, if the citizens or the clan dislike their burdens and say, "Go ahead and do what you want; it’s fine if you don’t do it," what will happen?
If that’s the case, it’s the end of it.
If you’re carrying all that baggage and you say you’re not going to move it, what will happen? If that tribe or that nation, which is responsible for its own baggage, decides to carry not only its own but also others’ baggage, what will happen? If God exists, what would He do? He would say, “Hurry up, get it done!” 
If the American people have a mountain of baggage and they say, “I don’t know about that baggage!” and just throw it away, and a small country like Korea says, “Oh, that’s great. We’ll take responsibility for it all,” what would happen? What would God do? Would He say not to call it America’s baggage? He would tell them to hurry up and carry it. That’s how it is. It will definitely happen that way. 
Korea may have a nation, but what about those who don’t have a nation? If the oppressed black people gather and say, “Oh, we’ll do what the nation can’t do,” and they keep crying and working hard, what will happen after one year, two years, three years? God would say, “Alright, then go ahead and try.” If that happens, that person will be given the privilege to carry the burdens of the entire world before God at any time. They will become a specific nation. 
In today’s world, in the miserable situation where everyone opposes the Unification Church, even the black people oppose it, if this Unification Church, which has nowhere to go, says, “I will take on this burden,” what will happen? Will God say, “No, you can’t do that”? Would He be surprised and open His mouth in astonishment? There are white people, black people, yellow people, and people of all colors gathered together; would He say it’s unbelievable? Even if God says that, we must say, “No, we will do it.” Then wouldn’t God also have no choice but to say, “Well, go ahead and try”? 
Now, if you’ve taken on this burden, are you just going to look at it, or are you going to carry it? (Laughter) Are you going to carry it until your legs hurt? Are you going to carry it until tears come out of your eyes? “Yes.” For how many hours? For how many years? “For a lifetime.” It’s easy to say “for a lifetime,” but will you eat when it’s time to eat, sleep when it’s time to sleep, wear clothes when it’s time to wear them, get married, have children, and then just throw all that away? What will you do? Is it the first thing or the last thing? “The last thing.” Is that true? “Yes.” So, here are young women close to 30 years old; do they want to get married or not? “I don’t want to get married.” (Laughter) When they say “no” and “yes,” what is it, the middle ground? (Laughter) They all know. They know exactly what they need to do. (Laughter) 
Everyone thinks, “Oh, I should get married first. I should get married first. Ah, it would be better to do it together with my husband after getting married.” (Laughter) 
So, what has more value: carrying the burden while loving each other or carrying it without love? “The first one.” Is that really true? “Yes.” They all know. (Laughter) Then, what about the person who eats while carrying the burden versus the person who doesn’t eat while carrying it? Which is better? “The one who doesn’t eat while carrying it.” And what about the person who doesn’t sleep and stays up all night carrying it versus the person who sleeps well and carries it? Which is better? “The one who doesn’t sleep while carrying it.” They all know. Even if this is analyzed scientifically, the same results will come out. 
This is the path of destiny for the Unification Church that cannot be avoided. 
Let’s say there is a person who is the most greedy. What would happen if that person were Reverend Moon? (Laughter) Greed is bad, but when the entire world is something that “I will do,” and then they say to God, “God, give me everything You want to do,” what would happen? At that moment, God would be surprised and say, “Oh, there’s such a person?” (Laughter) If that person is Reverend Moon, what do you think would happen? Would God say, “Go ahead and try”? Absolutely, God would say to try. But what if they are responsible for the burdens of the world and the burdens of heaven, and they face opposition from both the world and the spiritual realm? Would they still do it? 
So, God is letting them try. They absolutely do not give up. If they proceed like a greedy leader, saying, “If you want to oppose, go ahead and oppose,” the more they are opposed, the greater God’s interest becomes.
Then, personally, they are better than the individuals of the world, and in terms of families, they are better than the families of the world. Even if Korea opposes, they are better than the Korean people, and even if Asia opposes, they are better than the Asian people. And even if the people of the world oppose them when they come to America, if they push through, what will God do? Would God say that they are a detestable person? What would He do? At that time, would He say that you did well to be greedy or that you did poorly? Would He say that greed was necessary or bad? “It was necessary.” (Laughter) That’s right. When this work is completed, He will say, “Ah, that was a wonderful greed.” 
Then what will happen? Will the Unification Church followers feel sympathy? Will they say, “What’s the point of doing this for their own benefit, what’s sympathy?” They will feel sympathy. 
Will you complain to God, saying, “Why do You make us carry such a burden and suffer? If You had left us alone, we would have lived well; what is this?” You all would do that, right? Isn’t that so? “No.” Then, are you the ones who praise Reverend Moon and like him? “Yes.” Yes, yes, yes… I can’t believe that answer. (Laughter) 
Let me ask you something. Has anyone among you ever thought, “Oh, I wish I hadn’t heard the Principle in the Unification Church…”? “Oh, if I hadn’t heard the Principle, I wouldn’t have lived this way, but now I can’t escape it, I can’t get away from it…”? (Laughter) Have you all thought that? Have you thought that? “Yes.” (Laughter) But does your “yes” mean that you like the teacher? (Laughter) And these days, when you go out on the street, when people talk about this and that, does it sound good to you? “Yes.” What does “yes” mean? When you call people “moonies,” do you say, “Oh, moonies”? When they say “moonies,” do you think, “What is a moonie?” and dislike it? You would be like that. 
So, what happens if you just leave it alone? If you just leave it alone, will you carry this burden? What do you think? When you look at human nature, is there anyone who likes to carry burdens? Not a single person. So, do you think the burden will be carried? Think about it. Do you want to carry it? “Yes.” What do you mean by “yes”? “I want to carry it.” These people. “I want to carry it!” (Laughter) 
So, inevitably, you need a leader who will hit you with a stick and make you go. You need a leader who, even when you’re playing, makes you feel scared and embarrassed enough to hide when they show up. Do you think such a person is needed or not? Think about yourself. “It’s needed.” You need someone who nags you and makes you unable to move and manages you. 
Would you prefer a leader who, when you meet them, is funny and dances and wants to play, or someone who pushes you to work, saying, “Work, work”? (Laughter) Which person do you prefer? “The one who pushes.” Is that really true? “Yes.” That’s how it is. 
This is the destiny of the Unification Church. Destiny is something that cannot be avoided. It’s a destiny that cannot be avoided. You have to make excuses after doing it first. You have to speak after doing it. You must fulfill your responsibilities before eating, before sleeping, and before resting. Is that a good way to lead and manage, or a bad way? “It’s a good way.” Then, do you do it because you can’t, or do you do it because you’re happy? “Because I’m happy.” 
You must be willing to give up everything for humanity and work hard. 
Now, let me ask you one more thing. While you are working now, is the work you are doing overwhelming? Is it easy or hard? “It’s easy.” Would you prefer to have one command a day, or three commands a day? “Three commands.” Raise your hand if you want three commands. Now raise your hand if you don’t want them. You want to raise your hand but can’t, so you’re doing this. (Laughter) They all know. The teacher knows all your circumstances well. There’s nothing he doesn’t know. 
Now, from a democratic perspective, if we didn’t step forward, we wouldn’t know, but if we’ve stepped forward to work, should we do it or not? “We should do it.” Then why the complaints? Why are you tired and saying, “Oh, I can’t go. I can’t go”? “Oh, I have to leave the Unification Church. I have to pack my bags…”? You all have thought about packing your bags. You’ve all thought like that. I know that well. But even if you pack your bags, you have nowhere to go… (Laughter) The Unification Church is not only in America. It exists everywhere in the world. Even in the southern tip of Africa, it exists. If you don’t want to believe in the Unification Church in Japan and go to England, within a year, you will meet a Unification Church member in England and get caught up again. (Applause) 
Just know this one thing. If running away were possible, the clever, witty, and proactive Reverend Moon would have run away first. (Laughter) No matter how far you go, there’s nowhere to go. There’s only this one hole. (Laughter) So we are bound to the same path of destiny. Since the teacher has felt what you feel in your heart, he knows everything. What you are doing, I have done it all. I have even played the beggar while getting food. I have entered all the dens of gangsters. Therefore, I can relate to anyone I meet. 
That’s why I am doing what no one else in the world can do. No matter who I meet from all walks of life, I understand their circumstances and feelings well. Do you see the teacher that way? Do you see it that way? “Yes, we do.” That’s why I can lead you. Even if the young ones try to slip away like eels, I can catch them all… 
So, will the Unification Church be able to bear the burden of destiny, or will it stop along the way? Let’s discuss what you will do. “We will bear it.” Is that really true? “Yes.” The American people have many difficulties. They dislike being controlled. Is that true or not? “That’s true.” What is the most difficult for me? When they say, “Oh, let’s do it” in front of the teacher, but when they go back to New York and just eat three meals, they change again. (Laughter) That’s why, as soon as I come to New York, I have to say, “You promised!” and do this. (Applause) Is that a good thing or a bad thing? Speak honestly. “It’s a good thing.” They know it well. 
That’s why I told Mr. Park and Joong-hyun, “Hey, do it this way.” You all came to New York well. Somehow, I have to make you work, and somehow, I have to push you into the organization so that you can’t move. Is that something you dislike, or something good? Is it something you dislike but is good? What is it? “It’s good.” 
That’s why I made the tall guy, Gay Hat, the doorkeeper. Do you like looking at Gay Hat’s face? Does just seeing his face make you feel bad, or does it make you feel good? (Laughter) Tell me. Did I set him up well or not? “You set him up well.” You all said he was set up well. 
Then why are you complaining? I hear all the complaints you make. (Laughter) You need to go out into the world and work. You need to carry this burden. Those who complain are people who have no responsibility and just drift away without work. Isn’t that right? “Yes.” You should do it more strongly and more quickly. 
Carry all the burdens, lie down in a big “大” shape, and let’s see if we can sleep so deeply that the house shakes while snoring. (Laughter) Let’s see if the people in New York can’t sleep because of the snoring of the people here. Let’s see if we can sleep so sweetly and deliciously that we forget to go to the bathroom and end up doing everything in bed. (Laughter) Those who don’t know might not understand, but I know all that. Let’s work and play once. In New York, let’s open all the doors to our wind and play so much that we can’t work. Let’s see if everyone in New York can play so much that no one can work. The teacher knows how to play too. (Laughter. Applause) 
But there is a responsibility. For humanity, you must throw away everything. Why must you do that? Because then the people of the world will all sympathize, and heaven will sympathize even more. The more miserable and difficult it is, the more you can gather the hearts of all humanity and the feelings of all humanity. 
You must be willing to do things that feel like dying while still being alive. 
Do you want to rise up after joining the Unification Church, or do you want to go down? “I want to rise up.” That’s good. Do you want to rise in a straight line, or do you want to rise in a winding way? “In a straight line.” They all know. Then are you rising in a straight line? Now, if it’s a bullet, is it better to go straight or to go winding? “Straight.” Is that how you all feel? You all want to go this way, right? “Yes.” When it’s time to eat, do you have to go down a little, and when it’s time to sleep, do you have to go down a little? Even if it’s the Unification Church, this is the principle… Do you go down when you sleep and when you eat? “That’s not true.” 
Then do you sleep for the sake of work, and do you eat for the sake of work? Do you have time to daydream? “No.” You don’t have that either. You must go with the will. Outside of the will, there is no room for thought. You can’t think about the house you used to live in or the person you used to love. “My eyes have become straight because of the will. My ears have become straight because of the will. My heart has become straight because of the will. My body has become straight because of the will.” That’s how it should be. Has it become that way? Even if I can’t fly, I must think that I will draw a straight line. “Even if I sleep, I sleep as a person who goes straight.” Is that how it is? 
Even when you go to the bathroom, do you say, “Oh, I’m going to the bathroom to work, to fulfill the will”? Is that how you think? Because there’s no time, do you say, “Hurry up, hurry up, you rascal!”? Do you think like that? “Yes.” (Laughter) If you think like that, would God say, “You rascal!” and hit your head, or would He say, “That’s commendable”? What would He think? Think about that. When God sees that, would He say it’s because you’ve been brainwashed, or what would He think? The teacher has done all this without thinking about success or anything else. As a result, he is said to have succeeded and to be a great person.
Alright, ladies, when you get married, do you want a husband like a teacher, or do you want a husband who is not like that? "Like a teacher." If you get a husband like me, you'll be unhappy. "That's not true." Whenever I go out first and say, "Honey, come out, come out, come out," you have to follow me, and it's always like that. Is that good? "Yes." (Laughter) Ask your mother. (Laughter) While putting on clothes, while putting on a coat, you just rush out.... Would a teacher have time to dress you? I'm busier.... (Laughter) Is that happiness? "Yes!" (Laughter) Even our kids, who know nothing, think that their mom and dad are just wandering around and living this life. Isn't that unhappy? Is it unhappy? But they think, "Our mom and dad are the best mom and dad in the world." That's right. 

When you do things like this, when you do it selflessly, do you think the world will see it as wonderful or as garbage? "Wonderful." As time goes on, it becomes a subject of research, and as time goes on, people become more interested and start to follow. Do you think so? "Yes." But how heavy is this burden? Let's think about that. This burden is something that Judaism could not solve even after 4,000 years of sacrifice. Christianity, despite having so many martyrs and enduring all kinds of suffering for 2,000 years, has not been able to take responsibility. Even if we set aside humans who believe in religion, from God's perspective, this is something that has not been achieved even after tens of thousands of years. So, is it an easy task or a difficult one? "It's a difficult task." 

That's why how amazing are the people who say they will take on this difficult task? When you look at that task, whether it's you or me, everyone runs away. When someone asks, "Are you going to do this task and die?" if it only means that you will die after doing this task, many people would say they would do something as incredible as dying. So, you must prepare to do something as good as dying while still alive. Otherwise, you cannot think about this task. Do you understand what I mean? 

You need to realize that you have taken on such a tremendous task. The Unification Church has taken on something enormous and incredible. This is destiny. It is a destiny that cannot be separated. Do you think you will do that task? "Yes." 

Once you get over the peak, everything in your life will rise to that standard. From today, I will allow you to go out, but let’s be bound by this time of destiny. If anyone says they will come back in 10 years because this task is hard, I will let them go. I will permit you to go. "I won't go." Why not? (Laughter) You don’t want to go? "No." Why not? You don’t think that way? What do you dislike? I know everything. Do you dislike that? "Yes." Seeing that, I think you are clever. Why? Because you know that one year is worth a thousand years, right? Do you understand that? 

Now, you are crossing a big mountain pass while walking on flat ground. The time it takes to cross this is equivalent to tens of thousands or hundreds of millions of years. (As he writes on the board) By overcoming this one thing, this person enters this high world, this high realm. Just by that one hour of crossing the peak, everything in their life rises to that standard. The value increases. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." 

Have you seen Leon Spinks and Muhammad Ali fighting in the ring? "Yes." When Leon Spinks gets on the stage, he stretches out and does this.... Up to the 15th round, it’s just a brief period. Life Journey and Restoration through Indemnity
Life refers to one’s entire life, one’s life. You all know how difficult it is to understand this now. 
The life of a human being drawing a myriad of curves 
We humans live a day, go through a year, and develop our entire life based on that year. Through that process, you all change. You go through life from childhood to adolescence, youth, adulthood, and old age.
Based on that period, some people have a short period of happiness, while others have a long one; some have a short period of unhappiness, while others have a long one. Such differences draw a curve, moving like a sine curve. In the midst of that, as you live centered on issues like love…. Then you are born, and you also die. 
When you think about it this way, you all experience it, but can there be only joy in living as a human being? You cannot just say with your mouth, ‘I am happy. It’s good. I am glad.’ Listening also draws a myriad of curves, thinking is the same, and feeling is also the same. 
As you walk the path of life, your thoughts create all sorts of ups and downs. Even centered on just myself, without anyone else being involved, this is how it is; therefore, we humans cannot live alone. There are interpersonal relationships, social relationships, national relationships, and global relationships.
Now, centered on the Unification Church, the issue is how to connect the civilization of Asia with that of the West and how to connect the Asian races with the races of the world. There will be complex and diverse curves drawn here. The question is how to make this curve become a straight line. If you think this way, you can understand that even in living one’s life, the way we live changes with the complex changes in the environment, and the directions can diverge. When some good thing manifests as a force and some phenomenal action occurs, it must be given and received according to the laws of motion.

Sadness and Tears

Today's message will be 'Sadness and Tears.' 

There is no one in this world who likes sadness, and no one who likes tears. However, we know that there are many such things in human life and in today's historical era. 

God created the universe with joy, but due to human fall, God is sad. 

When God created the universe, was it to see the day of sadness first or the day of joy first? Without a doubt, it can be said it was to see the day of joy first. 

If we look at the Book of Genesis in the Bible, we know that God commanded everything created on the first day, second day... up to the sixth day to be good. Even after creating humans, He said, "It was very good." The word 'good' is achieved from a place that transcends sadness. 

Therefore, the beginning of creation also started from joy, and the fruits of creation should also bear joy, wouldn't that be the purpose of human creation? Starting from joy, going through all processes joyfully, and coming with the expectation of joyful results. 

However, everything depended on one person. So if humans are completed in joy, then this history, just like the history of creation, must be a continuous series of joy. When we think about the life of humans created in joy, Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden could have faced a joyful God, but we must recognize that Adam and Eve, who grew up in such an environment, faced a day of sadness, indicating that human history began as a miserable history. 

If we look at it that way, from the position of God, the master of this history of creation, the first master who could taste joy is also God. From God's perspective, the joy of establishing eternal ideals is unchangeable. Yet, this has changed. Therefore, in the historical era, God is the master of joy, but from the day of the fall, He is also the one who first felt sadness. 

Who among this earth or this universe shed tears first? Was it the fallen Adam and Eve, or God? "It was God." It cannot be otherwise. We must understand that God first felt sadness and shed tears. So, regarding the results of Adam and Eve's fall, when they were driven out of the Garden of Eden, Adam must have been sad then, and it was then that Adam shed tears. From that day on, humanity's history of sadness began, and the history of tears continued.

When you think like this, the existence of 'I' becomes a problem.

God's Presence and Path

Good morning! "Good morning." Everyone wishes to be happy. They want to rejoice in happiness. To be happy, to be joyful, one cannot do it alone. One cannot do it alone. Happiness is achieved in a relational context. The same goes for good things.

Happiness and joy only come from relational contexts. God is a good being. But can we say that God is a happy being? Can God be happy alone? Ultimately, God also needs a counterpart. For you to be joyful… You are seeking an exciting joy. You are seeking a stimulating joy. This is true for both men and women. It is the same for all people. We can conclude that just as people are the same, so is God. This applies to Eastern people, Western people, people of the past, present, and future. It is not true that only Eastern people are joyful while Western people are not.

Therefore, when considering this, what is the problem for everyone to be joyful? Here, we can hear words like war or struggle.

If one wins, the other… Just because one has won, we cannot eliminate the loser. The loser remains. The defeated ones do not simply want to disappear; they harbor the desire to retaliate. Heaven of Resurrection

You all know well that people around the world long for a day of happiness and an ideal world.

Heaven is a world where we live in true God's love.

Among people worldwide, many admire the "American people" and see living in America as their lifelong hope. However, America is not heaven. Therefore, the American people also have a historical destiny to seek a higher ideal world.

If heaven were realized, there would be no such thing as religion, including any Unification Church. Because heaven remains as a hope, we must understand that both God and humanity wish to go there and are being led to go there.

So how do we go to heaven? That is the question. The religions that have emerged until now are for the purpose of establishing heaven. When we say "heaven," there must be a nation, a nation. That nation must have sovereignty, a people, and territory.

On March 26, 1978, at the Belvedere Training Center.

* This message is also published in <Words> No. 209.

Who is the sovereign of that nation? God. Centered on our ancestors who were blessed by God from the beginning, the direct descendants of God will lead this historical heaven through the eternal lineage. That is a very ordinary and reasonable conclusion. What kind of people will the citizens be? The descendants connected through all the ancestors related to this lineage must be a global people woven together by brotherly ties and sentiments. Therefore, that sovereignty is not just the sovereignty of the firstborn but becomes the sovereignty of the brothers. Thus, the firstborn and the descendants will unite to form a nation that is one with God. And we must understand that this world, this earth, is its territory.

Under such sovereignty, the people living in harmony of love is heaven. What kind of love? It is a world where we live by true God's love, and we can conclude that this is the concept of heaven. That love is not false love. It is not the love spoken of in the fallen world. Because God is the center of love, that world is a world connected by true love. That love is not a powerless love that can be invaded by fallen beings; it is absolute love. We must understand that. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

Now, when we say "heaven of resurrection," what does resurrection mean? It means to live again. Why is resurrection necessary? Because we could not reach the place of heaven. Why could we not reach the place of heaven? Because we fell.

The fall is not limited to Adam and Eve alone; it is not. The existence that is the ancestor of humanity and the fundamental source has fallen, which means that not only the individual fall is involved but also the family, tribe, nation, and the entire world, the entire ideal of heaven has been destroyed. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Therefore, this world has fallen below the realm of the fall. It has fallen into a hellish world that is unrelated to the ideal world of heaven.

Now, from now on, how do we go to heaven? What is the biggest problem here? There is land. There are people. But what is missing? There is no love of God. The problem is simple. So the question of how to find God's love is a historical task. This remains as a significant problem that fallen humanity must solve. What remains as a problem? "God's love."

To go to heaven, we must become a family that eternally aligns with God's heart and love. That is not just God. That heart is not just God's heart. We must understand that humanity, all things, and everything are combined there. Why? Why is it all tied together? The fallen Adam is one person, but because Adam fell, he caused the emotional realm of God's heart, humanity's heart, and the universe to all be shattered.
The first is (while writing) that all things participated. Then, humans participated. There is something called the heart. There is something called heart (heart; 마음). Love participated in that. So, in the Unification Church, this is reduced to what is called "heart" (심정). Do you understand what I mean? The meaning of heart is different. Therefore, the hearts of all things must be the same as God's heart. The human heart must also be the same as God's heart. The three hearts must become one. 

Thus, the concept that humans must love all things has emerged. We must love all things. Then we must love people. After that, we must love God. To love, the heart must come first. We must carry love while prioritizing the heart. In our lives today, fallen humans, even if original humans had not fallen, should have done so, but fallen humans are using that as a standard and are going forward centered on this criterion. 

Now, does God's heart change? "No." If God's heart changes, then God's heart and love can also change. Do your hearts change or not? "They do." There is a Korean proverb that says human hearts change with the morning and evening, but the colors of the mountains and all green do not change. Eastern people change, but Western people, Americans, do not change, right? (Laughter) In fact, in some ways, Western people are more fickle. Why? That’s what I’m saying, let’s see what happens. If Reverend Moon does what he wants, will America fail or prosper? "It will prosper." It will prosper. I know them well, but they don’t know and oppose, and that’s the problem. Should we stop here? No. We must go forward strongly. Should we do it or not? "We must do it."

Everyone, have you been liberated from society or not? When you go down to the very bottom and come up like this, God cooperates with you. Does it happen like that? Then what happens? You have to meet them to know. You will know who is real when you meet them. Go meet the Black community, the Hispanic community, and the White community. Within an hour, even in 30 minutes, they will kneel down and say, "Oh, we were wrong." Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." That’s for sure. In 30 minutes to an hour… It won’t even take an hour. In 30 minutes, completely…. They are asking for evidence. If the Moonies are bad, they are asking for evidence. 30 minutes is long. You can completely turn them around in 3 minutes. So if you meet for just 30 minutes, everything will be resolved.

Now, the Unification Church is bad, but the Moonies are good. Reverend Moon is bad, but the Moonies are good, that’s the rumor. (Laughter) Reverend Moon is bad, but the Moonies are good. The Moonies are good. So Reverend Moon stays quiet, invisible, and only the Moonies go out. Do you understand? "Yes." Go to the streets of New York! Go anywhere! You Moonies, go! Save the American people! So what do you do? Become someone who can boast about being persecuted! Boast about being persecuted! Do you understand? Regarding the persecution of the Unification Church, the second generation will ask, "Why did those who are worse than Unification Church members persecute them?"

Now, is God a loving being or a merciless being? "He is a loving being." What makes Him a loving being? He is merciless towards the Unification Church. "No." Why not? When He didn’t know this principle, He was merciless, but when He knows this principle, He becomes a God of love. Why is He a God of love? To overcome this as individuals, we must go beyond individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world…. This is something you cannot achieve in a lifetime. All the parents are kidnapped, and everyone in the world, including the spirit world, is fighting together. There is no other way. So what does it mean? If I am not falling and it becomes quiet, then I have won. That’s the strategy. Do you understand? So you must know that it is God’s loving strategy to hand everything over at once because He loves us.

Thus, the more global the religion, the more destined it is to overcome global persecution. Therefore, when a global religion emerges and is persecuted globally, you should know that the time is near. You can draw that conclusion. Because it is a quick way to liberation, God uses that method. That is the secret to being liberated from society and the environment. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

So if you get tired of persecution and say, "Oh, not again…," that would be a big problem. You must endure confidently. Then, even if Satan opposes, it will be a loss for him, and there will be no need for further opposition. No matter how much he opposes, there is no possibility of winning. Do you understand what I mean? Satan tried to destroy Reverend Moon, but instead, he made Reverend Moon famous, and everyone became interested. Satan made that happen and thought, "Oh, it turns out this is a loss! What a disaster." Reverend Moon became globally famous. If there hadn’t been opposition, would he have become globally famous? (Laughter. Applause)

Because all the Whites are beating up on the Blacks, the Blacks and Hispanics all come to Reverend Moon. They all cling to me, leaving only the Whites. Do you understand! (Applause) Even if the Whites keep opposing, then the sons of the Whites will become our allies, the sons. Do you understand? Only the old oppose, and the young follow. Just wait and see. It’s certain. Heaven judges like this. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Is that happening or not? "It is happening." So are we failing or winning? "We are winning." You must know that.

To be liberated from the established church is to be able to be liberated from the world.
From now on, what the Unification Church must do is to go into the established church and fight with the old people there. "Why do you oppose Reverend Moon! Isn’t the established church of this old era wrong?" Then they will completely turn around. We are going into the established church to evangelize. When young Unification Church members go in to evangelize, the old people oppose the Unification Church, so the young people who come out of the established church will become our allies. That is a natural principle.

When the young people of the Unification Church evangelize, and the old oppose, the young people who come out of there will naturally become our allies. (Laughter) Now, to go to the established church, you first visit the homes of the people who attend the established church. Then you say, "Let’s compare you and us," and then go to the church and say, "Let’s compare your will with what God desires." That kind of game must be played. So now, 120 established churches are being sent out from the seminary. Do you know that? You all must play that game. You go to their homes before going to church. You must visit the church through their homes. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

Why do you go? Why must it be done this way? I must be liberated from the Christians and the established church to find a way to go to the world. That is the closest path, so it cannot be avoided. Do you understand? The good thing is that they are sick and now they are all about to fail and die. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." So when the day comes when they can be cured and healed, we can utilize that great thing globally. We will not lose what God has worked for over 2,000 years, we will establish all historical foundations, and we can do the work of establishing God’s prestige and the prestige of Jesus Christ who died.

Now look. Families in America, have you been liberated from the opposition of your parents? That’s right? And society is all coming to our side. Next, we must be liberated from the church, from the church. The church must say, "The Unification Church is good!" If we are liberated only from the church, is it easy or difficult to be liberated from America and the world? It will be easy. Liberation rights from not only America but from the entire world will be opened. Liberation rights from the entire world will emerge through the church, through Christianity. Liberation rights from the entire world will be achieved at once. And there will be the power to be liberated even from the communist world. Isn’t that right? Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

Do you want to do it or not? "We will do it." Why must it be done? Christianity holds the key to liberating the world. Therefore, to be liberated, we must do this.

New York is the frontline to determine global liberation rights.
So the teacher has directed all the scholars, our church theologians, smart and capable people, and now they are causing issues on the university campuses. You may be wondering, "What is the teacher doing?" but the teacher is not idling. The entire academic community is doing it now… If New York is good, then if New York turns around, all of America will turn around. San Francisco, Boston, Chicago, Atlanta, Philadelphia, they will all turn around. It will happen all at once. So it is the frontline, the frontline. You must know that New York is the frontline.

What does "York" mean? What does "York" mean! What does the "York" in New York mean! I think of "oak tree" as "York." What does that mean? The oak tree is a very strong tree. If New York turns around, the whole world will collapse. That’s right. Do you know such things?

Ah, why is it Manhattan? What is this egg-like thing? It’s a ship, a ship. No matter how big the ship is, it will sway left and right. Right now, it is loaded with a lot of cargo, and if one more person gets on, it will sink. So when our Unification Church says "bang," the Old York will sink, and the Liberation York will rise. (Applause)

However, because everyone dislikes the Unification Church members, when we try to board, they want to jump off. (Laughter) Because the Unification Church members have come in and stirred things up, they say, "Oh, I want to escape from New York." If that happens, they will survive. Wherever you go, it’s the Unification Church, and wherever you go in high-rise buildings, even if you take the elevator, anywhere you go, they will say, "Oh, I don’t want to see the Moonies, I want to pack my bags and leave." Then they will survive.

Until now, Whites have left American cities because they didn’t want to see Blacks, but now they are leaving because they don’t want to see the Moonies. When they see it, Blacks, Whites, and Asians all leave because they don’t want to see the Moonies. So even the Blacks are packing their bags and leaving. Then the ship will rise, and after that, it will become a new New York, that’s what I think. Do you understand! "Yes."

So let’s go around every valley day and night! We must go around and do that. "In this house, there is a TV, and in that house, there is a cassette, so since the Moonies are teaching, I must run away because I don’t want to see the Moonies." When the atmosphere is created like that, you must know that New York will completely revive. When New York revives, America revives, and when America revives, the world revives. Then people from Europe and all over the world will be drawn to New York. Will you do it or not? "We will do it." Why, why must it be done? "Because Christianity holds the string of liberation from the world." Therefore, to be liberated, we must do this.

This fight is to represent the global liberation rights determined in New York. The greatest fight to establish liberation rights centered on a single destination in history, between the spiritual world and the physical world, is the fight of the Unification Church and New York. You must know that the fight here in New York is focused all the way to the spiritual world. It’s not that we are dead and fighting in the spiritual world, but we are engaging the spiritual world in this fight, standing at the historical frontline of God’s providence. This is what we are doing to liberate the realm of Satan, to liberate myself.

You must understand that this is happening in a place where people from all countries gather. There is no other place in the world like New York. New York is a small island that you can reach in 15 minutes by car, and you can cross it in less than 5 minutes. God has gathered people from all over the world here, making it the center of world culture, and I believe that He has prepared this for the Unification Church. New York is the key to liberating the world and us.

Here is the Hudson River! Hudson River. When you hear "Hudson," what do you think? "It’s a hot son." That’s what you think. (Laughter) It’s hot. (Laughter) You are supposed to feel the heat right away. That’s how I think. So everyone, who is the hot son? Are you the hot son? "Yes." Whose hot son is it? Is it Satan’s hot son or God’s hot son? "It’s God’s." You like that! "Yes."

When I hear "river," I think of revival. I think of revival. When I hear "river," I get the impression of "a resurrected person." So when you say "hot son river," I think, "Ah, it’s a resurrected person to become a hot son." (Applause) Do you understand?

This New York has become Old York, Old York. We are truly making a new New New New York through resurrection, growth, and completion. (Laughter) Why did I buy the New Yorker Hotel? "Because it’s the home of New Yorkers, so I bought it happily." That’s how I think. Now that we have prepared a home for New Yorkers, I think all New Yorkers will come to us. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." A New Yorker must save the New Yorkers.

Why do you live here in New Yorker? Do you live here for convenience in urinating and looking back? "No." Why do you live here? Why? You live here to become a hot son and to revive New York. Do you understand? "Yes." Eating is for that reason. Sleeping is for that reason. Believing in the Unification Church is for that reason. Needing Reverend Moon is for that reason. That’s why I settled in New York. To indemnify everything…. This is the core place that compresses the world the most, the core place where humanity lives, and because there are many complicated issues and various problems here, I have settled here. Isn’t that right? Is that correct or not? "That’s correct." When New York turns around, the world will turn around. Isn’t that true? Therefore, New York must be difficult. It must not be easy. Because it’s difficult, it has global value. It must be difficult. Here we must create the conditions for heavenly liberation. Then we will liberate the nation and the world. From that point on, it will be about receiving liberation and liberating others.

In this regard, we must recognize that God has given us a good battlefield throughout history. The good battlefield that God has given as the final gift to the Unification Church is New York. Do you understand what that means? "Yes."

If we win in New York, the conditions to win everything will be established.
So, will you win with your hands or not? "We will win." If that happens, because of you, God will win, the spiritual world will win, the world will win, and all of America will gain the authority to win. If New York only holds the thought of our Unification Church, everything will be completely resolved. Isn’t that right? "Yes." (Applause)

Recently, I heard rumors that Radio City is closing down, and I thought, "That’s good. That’s good. Soon, they should close down New York City Hall too." That’s what I think. In the future, who will…
Are you going to take over the city! If you become the mayor, it will be a big problem. The wages keep getting raised, and the gap keeps widening, so now it’s a mess. Since you raised the salaries of the New York City Hall employees under your jurisdiction, it’s only natural that you should raise the wages of the general public as well, and so you keep raising them, and the problems keep arising.

What is the name of the current mayor of New York? "It's Koch." When you say 'Koch,' in Korean, it sounds like '까치' (magpie). (Laughter) When you say 'Carter,' it means that Carter becomes a subject of controversy. (Laughter) Just wait and see. So, who can be the owner of New York? Is the Rockefeller Foundation the owner of New York? "No." Who is the owner, then? "You, teacher." Why am I the owner? You all, you are the owners of New York. Do you understand? "Yes." Since you are the owners, you need to be active. You need to be active morning and night. You need to be active after lunch, after breakfast, you need to be active. Act like the owners.

You should go into any house and relieve yourselves. People only eat, sleep, and relieve themselves; that’s all there is to it. Human life consists of coming and going, eating and sleeping, and then good and bad; these are the six aspects of human life. Is there anything that doesn’t fit into that? Right? So, who do I come and go for? For God. Who do I eat and sleep for? For God. And who do I experience good and bad for? For God. That’s all there is. How many aspects are there to human life? Coming and going, then eating and sleeping, then good and bad…. That’s all there is. Do you understand what I’m saying? "Yes."

What do you do after eating? You go out, right? Then what do you do when you come back? You sleep. And then what? There are good and bad things, right? That’s life. Meeting someone good, meeting someone unpleasant, eating with someone you love, and so on…. Isn’t that right? If you think about it, life is simple. If you think simply, everything is simple. Now you understand, right? "Yes." 

You eat and sleep here. And you come and go here too. Good and bad are also here. Right? "Yes." Who is that because of? "Because of God."

So, do you want to be liberated from New York, or not? Do you leaders of the Unification Church want to be liberated from New York? "No." What is it? Do you want to be liberated from New York, or not? "We do not want to be liberated." Then where do you want to be liberated from? Didn’t I say that New York is the core representing all the countries of the satanic world?

If we organize a band of about 3,000 people, with 1,000 in the north, 1,000 in the central, and 1,000 in the south, and we go ‘bang, bang, bang,’ won’t Manhattan shake? "Yes." How simple is that, and how small is this world? Then when they hear, ‘What is this? This is the sound of a band calling all New Yorkers to come out,’ will New Yorkers want to come out or not? Should they open the doors and welcome, or should they curse and say, ‘You idiots!’? "They should welcome." Has it become like that now? "No." When will it be like that? If you leave it alone, do you think it will happen in a thousand or ten thousand years? "No." Then when? When will you do it? "Now." Do you really want to do it? "Yes."

So, what day is it today? "It’s April 1st." When you say ‘April 1st,’ what does that mean? It means a quarter of understanding has passed. You all think, ‘Since a quarter of the important year 1978 has passed, what will happen when 1978 is over? Oh, I hope 1978 passes quickly. A quarter has passed, so three-quarters are left. Hurry up. Pass quickly.’ Right? "No." How is it? Are you worried and thinking, ‘Oh no, this is a big problem,’ or are you thinking, ‘Oh, I feel good’? "I think it’s a big problem."

When June and July come, the rainy season will come. After May passes, when will we work and when will we fight? It’s already April, soon to be May. The demonstrations happening in New York are opposing our Unification Church, and they are only making our <News World> look good. (Applause) It’s a very pleasant thing. Why isn’t <News World> demonstrating? (Laughter) Those people demonstrate for money, for themselves. They are different from you. They boast in normal times, but we boast in extraordinary times. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." The American people are so relaxed that they don’t even think about fearing communism, but we feel the threat of communism and fight against it.

So, do you want to do it in April and May, or not? Do you want to try it, or not? "We will do it." Who are you doing it for? "For God." If you fight like that, you will have the conditions for liberation. If you have that, you will be liberated in America and liberated in the world. So, you will be liberated as individuals, and then liberated in the world…. If you are liberated only in New York, then in the spirit world, liberation will happen automatically. I know that if we win in New York, the conditions for liberation from everything will be established. Think of it as standing in a historical battlefield with significant meaning and fight like a warrior.

Moreover, why are we demonstrating on April 1st? Why are we making a fuss after being quiet all this time? It’s because the time to lay the foundation for the second generation has begun. Because of this time, we must start a simultaneous attack both internally and externally. So, as representatives of heaven, men and women who represent the past, present, and future, let us attack in this historically significant April! We must resolve to do this. So, shall we do it, or not? "We will do it." Then let’s raise our hands and swear before heaven.

The return to New York will be through the home church movement using video and cassette tapes. Now, I will give special instructions. I have specifically instructed Kamiyama to bring in 300 TV sets and video sets as soon as possible. So, what we will do is, since we have about 1,000 people living in New York, we plan to distribute one set to every three people. This is not just talk; it’s practical. You all have areas where you have been assigned 360 homes, right? You have been assigned, right? "Yes."

Right! "Yes." Do you understand what I’m saying? "Yes." Focus on 300 people and start the home church immediately. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Therefore, within the two months of April and May, you must lay the foundation for the home church so that these three people will split into three from the beginning of June. By that time, we will prepare 600 TV sets. So, we will give one to each area with 360 homes. And by the end of the year, we will plan to expel everyone who was here to that area. We plan to send everyone out starting in September. Do you understand what I mean? You must establish a foundation where you can eat and sleep responsibly. Do you understand? "Yes."

And you must send one person to each New Yorker’s home. Then you will train them. You will send them out for street witnessing and have them do all kinds of movements in the city. The cleaning movement will start from that new person to revive the city. So, we are thinking about how to sustain these 1,000 people, up to 5,000 people.

Then, 1,000 home churches will become 3,000, 5,000 home churches, and if we can create that by June next year, I believe New York will have a solid foundation for complete liberation. When that day comes, if ten people are in one home church, it will scientifically result in 50,000 people. Do you understand what I’m saying? "Yes." This is what we are doing. Do you understand? We will create home churches and starting in September, we will send you out. We will not give you the keys here. We will establish bases there. Do you understand what I’m saying? "Yes." This is not just talk. It’s not just talk.

So, will we do it or not? "We will do it." We cannot not do it. We cannot not do it. So, when there are more than 40 members in a home church, I will tour by car. If anyone doesn’t want to do that, they should withdraw now. Is there anyone? Will everyone do it? "Yes." When that day comes, everything will be resolved.

Now, we have prepared video tapes that can be used for ten hours, twenty hours, even for training sessions. (Applause) I’m not asking you to lecture. If you play it every day, you will memorize it completely. If you play it day and night, even if your head is like a tofu bag or a bean bag, you cannot help but remember. (Laughter) Then when I whisper, you will all follow along. When it comes to that, if I move your hearts, you will follow along. If I make a joke, you will joke back, and everyone will completely follow along. (Laughter) Then after that, if I turn it off and say, ‘Next, I will do it. I will do it this way, so listen, it’s delicious,’ you will be able to say it even better. So, do you think it will work, or not? "I think it will work." Then no matter how much the <New York Times> makes a fuss and opposes, it will not matter. New Yorkers will automatically know.

Kamiyama! "Yes." Order the video tapes quickly, one for each of the three people, quickly. Kamiyama, order quickly. Do you understand what I’m saying? "Yes." After you receive that, go and explain everything and persuade them to get a house and set it up there.

And you, your mothers and fathers, I told Kamiyama to make cassette tapes, so I will send those to the parents. I will send them, so you should teach them all with that. You must teach them. Also, distribute cassette tapes to those in the neighborhood who oppose and tell them to listen to it first, and then oppose it. Even if the parents say not to do it, you will do it.

And Kamiyama! "Yes." Kamiyama, organize a mobile unit equipped with TV and video tape sets of the May 16th Plaza event, the Washington event, the Madison Square Garden event, etc. Gather the parents and have them lecture. (Applause) You need to prepare for that.

To carry out this movement, we are currently making quite a few cassette tapes. So, send those out today; there are three two-hour cassette tapes, so send them quickly to the parents. We will do this movement, so don’t oppose it; just get to know it first and then oppose it, and send it quickly. Some people are already writing letters to prepare for this movement and sending them all out. Do you understand what I’m saying? "Yes."

Then if the parents ask you, ‘Oh, send more,’ you will charge them 50 cents each, so they will pay $1.50. If their parents want to order thirteen sets, they will prepare $15 and send those thirteen sets to distribute to their friends. This is the movement we are doing. If you send three for $1.50, that will be six hours, so send three for $1.50, and if their parents want more, you will fundraise to buy and send them.

Look, when you go back to your hometown and say, ‘I will show you the amazing wedding film of 1,800 couples, which is unparalleled in the world, so come,’ you will see that friends and relatives will gather. If you say, ‘I will show you the best film in the world, which is only once,’ everyone will come. (Applause) Why is that? Of course, parents are interested, but especially young people, those who are not married, are more interested. (Laughter) This is all part of a psychological operation plan. I expect a tremendous response. Do you understand? "Yes."

So, what is your home? Your home becomes the home church. When it becomes the home church, then you will save your relatives and clan all at once. From the first day your parents hear about the Unification Church, they become the home church leaders, your parents. So, if there are good pictures of the Unification Church, show them, and let them hear all the teachings; you can do that as much as you want. Then you can also create good films to show, and show performances by famous orchestras, famous singers, and famous violinists. Do you understand what I’m saying? "Yes."

Now, you have entered a stage where you can carry out such movements in earnest, and you are doing the home church movement here. And you will coach your parents when you go home. You will coach them on how to do the home church movement. Then you will be told to restore your clan. So, this is a matter directly connected to you. You must take what you have won here and go back to your hometown to save it.

If you establish a representative for the home church here, then you will go back to your hometown. You must achieve rebirth, growth, and completion. (Applause) This is not just talk. This is what you will do. By around June next year, I will tell everyone to pack their bags and go home. I will make cassette tapes to send out. Do you understand? "Yes." So, if you promote the home church movement to your parents and they welcome it, then when you ask them to send you, they will immediately send you. Then, as the touring company goes around promoting, if they want it there, they will keep sending you.

That is what your parents will want. With a good color TV, a video tape set, and ten cassette tapes, that will be a great pride in that neighborhood. Then, if you keep showing movies, like performances by famous orchestras, the response will improve immediately. Do you understand what I’m saying? "Yes."

You might wonder, ‘Will New York be empty?’ but absolutely not. We are also doing the home church movement here. Quickly saving your hometown is the secret to creating the kingdom of heaven on earth. Restoring families, centering on families, is the secret and principle of creating the kingdom of heaven on earth, so you will return to your hometown and become the messiah of your hometown. This is the way of the principle.

Then what will happen to your parents? Until now, they have all opposed it, but now they will boast about it. Your parents and siblings will say, ‘Look at our son who has become a true person,’ and they will proudly walk around the neighborhood waving flags 24 hours a day. This will definitely happen. Do you understand? "Yes." Those who succeed in the home church movement will not send their children home alone; they will bless them before sending them, and that is the thought of the teacher. (Applause)

Let us restore New York and our hometown through the home church movement. Now, if you want to do it, do it; if you don’t want to do it, then don’t. If you can’t do it, I will bring in people from Guatemala and Asia to do this work.
Bring in Black people and bring in Hispanic people. Do you understand?  
"Yes."  
How long will you be here? "Until June next year." So in June next year,  
you all have to go back to your hometowns. Now, since we have won, we have to go back to our hometowns after fighting on the front lines and winning. Isn't that right? You want to go back to your hometown, right? "Yes." Now, do you understand? So I say, "Anora!" Now, I will do the home church movement here in New York, and then I will go back to my hometown and return home! Do you understand? "Yes."  
So, starting from June, all of you will go out for the home church movement. Prepare until May, and from June, you will definitely go out. You will go out and then by September, everyone must be replaced one by one. So we need to create a strong organization here and train. We need to do street propaganda, hold demonstrations, and engage in strong movements; we need to do all sorts of activities. So we have to make it so that "New York has become the land of Moony. Moony. Moony." (Applause. A brief comment was made to Kamiya in Japanese, but it could not be recorded due to poor audio quality.)  
So, shall we do it or not? "Let's do it." Shouldn't we create some work? What will come of this? Even here, we pay for our meals. So, it will be the same there; we will pay for our meals and stay while doing the home church movement. We will go to work from there. Every day, while going to work, prepare to return to your hometown quickly. Do you understand? "Yes."  
And if possible, quickly bring your younger siblings here to train them, so they can take your place. Do you understand? "Yes." This applies not only to church members but also to company members and newspaper members; there are no exceptions. So, after returning to your hometown, you will all lay the groundwork, and then you will go out to the global stage, to foreign countries. Since everyone in America knows the Unification Church, then you will all go abroad. That’s how we will develop. So when you go out into the world, the Unification Church will become invincible.  
If you want to teach according to the principles, you must work hard as you have been trained. When that day comes, development will happen just like that. Even if you are told not to evangelize, you will end up doing it. So, let’s have hope and from now on, starting today, April 1st, we must advance vigorously. Do you understand? "Yes."  
The body is made up of four parts. Do you know? The eyes, nose, mouth, and body are four parts, and the two legs and two arms are four parts, and the torso, lungs, heart, and stomach are four parts. We must mobilize the whole body and march forward. To achieve a hot revival... If you are tired and exhausted, go to the Hudson River and say, "River! I want to learn from you." Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."  
Let’s do it like lightning! Let’s do it quickly. Quickly! Kamiya, Sudo, Neil Salonen, everyone must do it. Do you support this? "Yes." If it doesn’t happen, you must pack your bags and leave. You have to quit. Then I won’t need to trust you, and I won’t need to live as a New Yorker. So, whether your face is good-looking or not, let’s try hard. Can’t you do that?  
Now, let’s stand up. Stand up and once again swear before God and give the order to start. From April 1st, we will launch an offensive in New York! (Three cheers. Applause)
